TEMPLATE 1: DRIVER ASSIGNMENT PACKET

TEMPLATE 4: FACILITY RULES SHEET
Template 4 of 7  |  
Generated / Autofill Output
Documents the specific rules, requirements, and procedures for a shipper or consignee facility — pulled from BOF route memory or captured during appointment scheduling. Provided to the driver before arrival. Designed as a reusable BOF facility-profile output.

BackOfficeFleet (BOF) — Driver and Dispatch Operations
TEMPLATE 5: DRIVER PROOF REQUIREMENTS SHEET
Template 5 of 7  |  
Generated / Autofill Output
One-page summary of all proof and documentation requirements for a specific load — tells the driver exactly what evidence to capture, when, and how to submit it. Consolidates proof requirements from the Rate Confirmation, Service Schedule, and customer / facility requirements.

BackOfficeFleet (BOF) — Driver and Dispatch Operations
TEMPLATE 6: DISPATCH RELEASE CHECKLIST
Template 6 of 7  |  
Editable Template
Final gate check completed by dispatch before releasing a driver to begin a load. This is the BOF Final Release Authorization — the last document reviewed before the driver departs. The Pre-Trip Readiness Summary (Template 2) confirms everything is in place; this checklist authorizes departure.
BOF Document Header Controls

BackOfficeFleet (BOF) — Driver and Dispatch Operations
TEMPLATE 7: DRIVER COMPLIANCE REMINDER / MISSING DOC NOTICE
Template 7 of 7  |  
Editable Template
Formal notice sent to a driver (or carrier, if owner-operator) when compliance documents are missing, expiring, or expired — used to prevent dispatch blocks and maintain DQF readiness.

•  
Triggers compliance tracking and expiration monitoring
•  
Triggers dispatch block when documents expire without renewal
•  
Triggers DQF status update
•  
Triggers communication log tracking
•  
Triggers settlement hold on affected loads if critical
•  
Triggers auto-escalation if unresolved past deadline
•  
Triggers command center watch for drivers with multiple open items
•  
Triggers dispatch release when all items resolved
Driver / Carrier Acknowledgment
"I acknowledge receipt of this notice and understand the deadlines for compliance. I will provide the required documents by the dates specified."
